### **Me** - 2017-07-26 12:36:56

Why be so easily disturbed? If you are well grounded in your own approval, free from errors in your judgement, then their insults hold no power over you. As it is, you are only teaching them how easy it is to hurt you, and now they must watch their steps even more closely. I believe you can in a moment free yourself from all such pain and future pains. Once you are grounded in the clarity of your own mind, it is easy to laugh off even the deepest insults since they are a reflection of the one giving them and not of you.

### **Mom** - 2022-01-09 15:28:54

Good morning Suzanne, 

My name is Krisy, I’m Jesses assistant. 
First I will make sure she sees your kind words, I know she will appreciate them 🥰

The tutorials are streaming only, we cannot do downloads as it is a streaming platform.  
BUT you can absolutely still do your painting party with your grand babies!! 

There are many options besides zoom for this.  If you have apple products like iPhone and iPods you can use those to do your tutorial over FaceTime. 

You can use Facebook messenger and share the screen while you paint.  

Also often times the zoom calls say 40 minutes but every time I’ve been on a zoom it’s been more than an hour. 

You can also create a Facebook group for you and your family and do a “party” they can log into the party when they go to the group and “join”. 

I hope this helps give you a variety of options:). 

I agree Jesse is a wonderful sunshine on a rainy day;).  

If you hit any bumps in the road that we can support you with please dot. Hesitate to reach out 😊.  

I hope you and your grandchildren have a lovely time painting!
